## Domain Knowledge (LLM-generated)
**Domain**: population ecology / population dynamics
**Analysis**: This task models population growth rate dP/dt as a function of time t and population P, which is the core problem of population dynamics. The inclusion of both t and P suggests possible non-autonomous dynamics such as time-varying carrying capacity or growth rates.

**Common formula structures in this domain**:
- Malthusian growth: dP_dt = c0 * P (exponential growth, unlimited resources)
- Logistic growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) (density-dependent growth with carrying capacity)
- Gompertz growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * log(c1 / P) (asymmetric sigmoidal growth)
- Theta-logistic: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) (generalized logistic with shape parameter)
- Allee effect (strong): dP_dt = c0 * P * (P - c1) * (1 - c2 * P) (growth with minimum viable population)
- Allee effect (weak): dP_dt = c0 * P * (P + c1) * (1 - c2 * P) (weak Allee effect modification)
- Logistic with harvesting: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) - c2 * P (density-dependent growth with proportional harvesting)
- Logistic with constant harvesting: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) - c2 (growth with constant yield harvesting)
- Time-varying carrying capacity: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P * (1 + c2 * sin(c3 * t))) (seasonal carrying capacity)
- Time-varying growth rate: dP_dt = c0 * (1 + c1 * sin(c2 * t)) * P * (1 - c3 * P) (periodic growth rate modulation)
- Richards growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) (flexible asymmetric growth curve)
- Beverton-Holt continuous: dP_dt = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) - c2 * P (density-dependent birth with linear death)
- Power-law density dependence: dP_dt = c0 * P - c1 * P**c2 (generalized density-dependent mortality)
- Exponential decay toward capacity: dP_dt = c0 * P * exp(-c1 * P) (growth rate exponentially suppressed by density)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Density-dependent feedback → multiplicative factor (1 - c*P) or (1 - (c*P)**n) representing resource limitation
- Allee effects (cooperative dynamics) → quadratic or higher-order terms in P with a positive interior root, e.g., P*(P - c1)*(c2 - P)
- Periodic environmental forcing → sinusoidal modulation of parameters: c*(1 + c1*sin(c2*t)) multiplying growth terms
- Harvesting or immigration → additive constant or linear terms independent of density-dependent structure
- Logarithmic growth suppression → log(c/P) factor as in Gompertz model, indicating growth rate proportional to log-distance from capacity
- Multiple stable equilibria → cubic or higher-order polynomials in P for dP/dt, creating multiple zero crossings
- Ratio-dependent effects → rational forms P/(c0 + P) representing saturating functional responses in self-limitation
- Delayed maturation or stage structure → terms involving t explicitly multiplied by population terms, representing cohort aging effects
